                <script>
                    jQuery(document).ready(function($){
                        var sNavContainer = '#site-navbar-container';
                        var sBodyContainer = '#main-body-container';
                        var sNavHeight = $(sNavContainer).height();
                        var iUnfixPoint = 0;
                        if( __tnt.client.platform.ios ){
                            $(sNavContainer).addClass('affix-sticky');
                        } else {
                            $sNavScroll = false;
                            $(window).on('scroll mousewheel', function(){
                                if( !$sNavScroll ){
                                    $sNavScroll = true;
                                    setTimeout(function(){
                                        var iFixPoint = $(sNavContainer).offset().top;
                                        var iCurrPoint = $(this).scrollTop();
                                        if( iCurrPoint >= iFixPoint && iCurrPoint > iUnfixPoint ){
                                            if( !$(sNavContainer).hasClass('affix') ){ 
                                                iUnfixPoint = iFixPoint;
                                                $(sNavContainer).addClass('affix').removeClass('affix-top');
                                                $(sBodyContainer).css('margin-top', sNavHeight+'px'); 
                                            }
                                        } else {
                                            if( !$(sNavContainer).hasClass('affix-top') ){ 
                                                $(sNavContainer).removeClass('affix').addClass('affix-top');
                                                $(sBodyContainer).css('margin-top', 0);
                                            }
                                        }
                                        $sNavScroll = false;
                                    }, 25);
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    });
                </script>

                        <script>
                            jQuery(document).ready(function($){
                                $('#followed-notification-modal-form').submit(function(e) {
                                    e.preventDefault();
                                    var $followBtn = $(this).find('.follow-btn');
                                    var sAction = $(this).attr('action') + '&title=' + $(this).find('.input-notification-name').val();
                                    $followBtn.find('.tnt-svg').show();
                                    $followBtn.prop('disabled', true);

                                    function submit_finished($alert){
                                        setTimeout(function(){
                                            $followBtn.find('.tnt-svg').hide();
                                            $alert.show().delay(2500).fadeOut(400);
                                        },2000);
                                    }

                                    $.ajax({
                                        type: 'POST',
                                        url: sAction,
                                        data: $(this).serialize(),
                                        success: function(oData){
                                            
                                            submit_finished( $('#followed-notification-modal-user .alert-success') );
                                        },
                                        error: function(oData){
                                            submit_finished( $('#followed-notification-modal-user .alert-danger') );
                                        }
                                    });
                                });
                            });
                        </script>

    <script>
        $(function(){
            /* handle automatic form expand */
            $('#search-form-text').focus(function(){
                $('#search-form-collapse').collapse('show');
                $('#search-form-collapse-toggle').toggleClass('collapsed');
            });

            $('#search-form-collapse').on('show.bs.collapse', function(){
                $('#search-form-collapse-toggle .advanced-text').addClass('hide');
                $('#search-form-collapse-toggle .close-text').removeClass('hide');
            });

            $('#search-form-collapse').on('hide.bs.collapse', function(){
                $('#search-form-collapse-toggle .advanced-text').removeClass('hide');
                $('#search-form-collapse-toggle .close-text').addClass('hide');
            });

            $('#input-type-all').change(function(){
                if(this.checked){
                    $('#input-type-articles,#input-type-collections,#input-type-videos,#input-type-images,#input-type-documents').prop('checked',false);
                }
            });
            $('#input-type-articles,#input-type-collections,#input-type-videos,#input-type-images,#input-type-documents').change(function(){
                if( $('#input-type-all')[0].checked ){
                    $('#input-type-all').prop('checked',false);
                }
            });
            $('.input-section-all').change(function(){
                if(this.checked){
                    $('.input-section').prop('checked',false);
                }
            });
            $('.input-section').change(function(){
                if( $('.input-section-all')[0].checked ){
                    $('.input-section-all').prop('checked',false);
                }
            });

            $('#input-d1, #input-d2').datepicker({
                startDate: '-100y',
                format: 'yyyy-mm-dd',
                todayHighlight: true,
                autoclose: 'true'
            }).on('show hide', function(e){
                e.stopPropagation();
            });

            $('#search-form').find('.search-submit').on(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function(){
                $('#search-form').submit();
            });
            

            $('#search-form').on('submit', function(){
                // Filter query
                var sQueryFiltered = $("#search-form input[name=q]").val().replace(/\?/g, '');
    $("#search-form input[name=q]").val( sQueryFiltered );
                
                // Define type and section values
                var sTypeVals = $.map($('.input-type:checked'), function(n, i){
                    return n.value;
                }).join(',');
                var sTypeValsSection = $.map($('.input-section:checked'), function(n, i){
                    return n.value;
                }).join(',');
                $('#input-t').val(sTypeVals);
                $('#input-c').val(sTypeValsSection);
                // Scrub empty inputs
                $(this).find(':input').each(function(){
                    if ($(this).val() == '') $(this).attr("disabled", "disabled");
                });
                // Sort by relevance patch
                $(this).find('#select-s option:selected')
                    .filter(function() {
                        return !this.value || $.trim(this.value).length == 0;
                    })
                    .parent()
                    .attr("disabled", "disabled");
                $('#search-form').find('.search-submit').find('[data-fa-i2svg]').replaceWith('<i class="fas tnt-spinner tnt-spin"></i>');
            });
        });
    </script>

<button onclick="topFunction()" id="myBtn" title="Go to top">Top</button><script>
// When the user scrolls down 20px from the top of the document, show the button
window.onscroll = function() {scrollFunction()};

function scrollFunction() {
  if (document.body.scrollTop > 20 || document.documentElement.scrollTop > 20) {
    document.getElementById("myBtn").style.display = "block";
  } else {
    document.getElementById("myBtn").style.display = "none";
  }
}

// When the user clicks on the button, scroll to the top of the document
function topFunction() {
  document.body.scrollTop = 0;
  document.documentElement.scrollTop = 0;
}
</script></div><div id="tncms-block-615295" class="tncms-block padding-bottom padding-left padding-top"><section id="block-615295" class="block emphasis-h3   " ><div class="block"><a href="/" ><img

                __tnt.googleEvent = function(obj) {
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.trigger',
                             'tncms.event.trigger.category': obj.category,
                             'tncms.event.trigger.action': obj.action,
                             'tncms.event.trigger.label': obj.label, 
                             'tncms.event.trigger.value': obj.value
                    });
                }
                /* Virtual page view */
                __tnt.googlePageView = function(obj) {
                    var sURL = obj.url.replace(/^.*\/\/[^\/]+/, '');
                    dataLayer.push({
                    
                        'event': 'tncms.event.virtual_pageview',
                            'tncms.event.virtual_pageview.url': sURL,
                            'tncms.event.virtual_pageview.title': obj.title
                    });
                }
                /* Social event */
                __tnt.googleSocial = function(obj) {
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.social',
                            'tncms.event.social.network': obj.network,
                            'tncms.event.social.action': obj.socialAction,
                            'tncms.event.social.target': obj.url
                    });

                <script>
                    jQuery(document).ready(function($){
                        var sNavContainer = '#site-navbar-container';
                        var sBodyContainer = '#main-body-container';
                        var sNavHeight = $(sNavContainer).height();
                        var iUnfixPoint = 0;
                        if( __tnt.client.platform.ios ){
                            $(sNavContainer).addClass('affix-sticky');
                        } else {
                            $sNavScroll = false;
                            $(window).on('scroll mousewheel', function(){
                                if( !$sNavScroll ){
                                    $sNavScroll = true;
                                    setTimeout(function(){
                                        var iFixPoint = $(sNavContainer).offset().top;
                                        var iCurrPoint = $(this).scrollTop();
                                        if( iCurrPoint >= iFixPoint && iCurrPoint > iUnfixPoint ){
                                            if( !$(sNavContainer).hasClass('affix') ){ 
                                                iUnfixPoint = iFixPoint;
                                                $(sNavContainer).addClass('affix').removeClass('affix-top');
                                                $(sBodyContainer).css('margin-top', sNavHeight+'px'); 
                                            }
                                        } else {
                                            if( !$(sNavContainer).hasClass('affix-top') ){ 
                                                $(sNavContainer).removeClass('affix').addClass('affix-top');
                                                $(sBodyContainer).css('margin-top', 0);
                                            }
                                        }
                                        $sNavScroll = false;
                                    }, 25);
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    });
                </script>

                        <script>
                            jQuery(document).ready(function($){
                                $('#followed-notification-modal-form').submit(function(e) {
                                    e.preventDefault();
                                    var $followBtn = $(this).find('.follow-btn');
                                    var sAction = $(this).attr('action') + '&title=' + $(this).find('.input-notification-name').val();
                                    $followBtn.find('.tnt-svg').show();
                                    $followBtn.prop('disabled', true);

                                    function submit_finished($alert){
                                        setTimeout(function(){
                                            $followBtn.find('.tnt-svg').hide();
                                            $alert.show().delay(2500).fadeOut(400);
                                        },2000);
                                    }

                                    $.ajax({
                                        type: 'POST',
                                        url: sAction,
                                        data: $(this).serialize(),
                                        success: function(oData){
                                            
                                            submit_finished( $('#followed-notification-modal-user .alert-success') );
                                        },
                                        error: function(oData){
                                            submit_finished( $('#followed-notification-modal-user .alert-danger') );
                                        }
                                    });
                                });
                            });
                        </script>

    <script>
        $(function(){
            /* handle automatic form expand */
            $('#search-form-text').focus(function(){
                $('#search-form-collapse').collapse('show');
                $('#search-form-collapse-toggle').toggleClass('collapsed');
            });

            $('#search-form-collapse').on('show.bs.collapse', function(){
                $('#search-form-collapse-toggle .advanced-text').addClass('hide');
                $('#search-form-collapse-toggle .close-text').removeClass('hide');
            });

            $('#search-form-collapse').on('hide.bs.collapse', function(){
                $('#search-form-collapse-toggle .advanced-text').removeClass('hide');
                $('#search-form-collapse-toggle .close-text').addClass('hide');
            });

            $('#input-type-all').change(function(){
                if(this.checked){
                    $('#input-type-articles,#input-type-collections,#input-type-videos,#input-type-images,#input-type-documents').prop('checked',false);
                }
            });
            $('#input-type-articles,#input-type-collections,#input-type-videos,#input-type-images,#input-type-documents').change(function(){
                if( $('#input-type-all')[0].checked ){
                    $('#input-type-all').prop('checked',false);
                }
            });
            $('.input-section-all').change(function(){
                if(this.checked){
                    $('.input-section').prop('checked',false);
                }
            });
            $('.input-section').change(function(){
                if( $('.input-section-all')[0].checked ){
                    $('.input-section-all').prop('checked',false);
                }
            });

            $('#input-d1, #input-d2').datepicker({
                startDate: '-100y',
                format: 'yyyy-mm-dd',
                todayHighlight: true,
                autoclose: 'true'
            }).on('show hide', function(e){
                e.stopPropagation();
            });

            $('#search-form').find('.search-submit').on(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function(){
                $('#search-form').submit();
            });
            

            $('#search-form').on('submit', function(){
                // Filter query
                var sQueryFiltered = $("#search-form input[name=q]").val().replace(/\?/g, '');
    $("#search-form input[name=q]").val( sQueryFiltered );
                
                // Define type and section values
                var sTypeVals = $.map($('.input-type:checked'), function(n, i){
                    return n.value;
                }).join(',');
                var sTypeValsSection = $.map($('.input-section:checked'), function(n, i){
                    return n.value;
                }).join(',');
                $('#input-t').val(sTypeVals);
                $('#input-c').val(sTypeValsSection);
                // Scrub empty inputs
                $(this).find(':input').each(function(){
                    if ($(this).val() == '') $(this).attr("disabled", "disabled");
                });
                // Sort by relevance patch
                $(this).find('#select-s option:selected')
                    .filter(function() {
                        return !this.value || $.trim(this.value).length == 0;
                    })
                    .parent()
                    .attr("disabled", "disabled");
                $('#search-form').find('.search-submit').find('[data-fa-i2svg]').replaceWith('<i class="fas tnt-spinner tnt-spin"></i>');
            });
        });
    </script>

<button onclick="topFunction()" id="myBtn" title="Go to top">Top</button><script>
// When the user scrolls down 20px from the top of the document, show the button
window.onscroll = function() {scrollFunction()};

function scrollFunction() {
  if (document.body.scrollTop > 20 || document.documentElement.scrollTop > 20) {
    document.getElementById("myBtn").style.display = "block";
  } else {
    document.getElementById("myBtn").style.display = "none";
  }
}

// When the user clicks on the button, scroll to the top of the document
function topFunction() {
  document.body.scrollTop = 0;
  document.documentElement.scrollTop = 0;
}
</script></div><div id="tncms-block-615295" class="tncms-block padding-bottom padding-left padding-top"><section id="block-615295" class="block emphasis-h3   " ><div class="block"><a href="/" ><img

        __tnt.trackEvent = function(obj) {
            if( jQuery.type(obj) === 'object' ){
                 
                    if(obj.category && obj.action){
                        __tnt.googleEvent(obj);
                    } else if(obj.network && obj.socialAction){
                        __tnt.googleSocial(obj);

                            app: obj.app,
                            metric: obj.metric,
                            id: obj.uuid
                        });

<script>/*<![CDATA[*/ 
                __tnt.googleEvent = function(obj) {
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.trigger',
                             'tncms.event.trigger.category': obj.category,
                             'tncms.event.trigger.action': obj.action,
                             'tncms.event.trigger.label': obj.label, 
                             'tncms.event.trigger.value': obj.value
                    });
                }
                /* Virtual page view */
                __tnt.googlePageView = function(obj) {
                    var sURL = obj.url.replace(/^.*\/\/[^\/]+/, '');
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.virtual_pageview',
                            'tncms.event.virtual_pageview.url': sURL,
                            'tncms.event.virtual_pageview.title': obj.title
                    });
                }
                /* Social event */
                __tnt.googleSocial = function(obj) {
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.social',
                            'tncms.event.social.network': obj.network,
                            'tncms.event.social.action': obj.socialAction,
                            'tncms.event.social.target': obj.url
                    });
                } /*]]>*/</script>
